<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-size: 10pt"></span></p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; width: 100%"><tr style="vertical-align: top; text-align: justify">
<td style="width: 0%"></td><td style="width: 0.7in; text-align: left"><span style="font-size: 10pt"><b>Item 8.01.</b></span></td><td style="text-align: justify; width: 90%"><span style="font-size: 10pt"><b>Other Events.</b></span></td>
</tr></table>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">On June 4, 2021 (the &#8220;Redemption Date&#8221;), The Coca-Cola Company
(the &#8220;Company&#8221;) redeemed all of the outstanding $1,354,734,000 aggregate principal amount of the Company&#8217;s 2.875% Notes
due 2025 (the &#8220;2.875% Notes&#8221;) under the Amended and Restated Indenture, dated as of April 26, 1988, as amended by the First
Supplemental Indenture, dated as of February 24, 1992, and the Second Supplemental Indenture, dated as of November 1, 2007, between the
Company and Deutsche Bank Trust Company Americas, as trustee.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">The 2.875% Notes were redeemed at a redemption price of 100% of the principal
amount of the 2.875% Notes, plus accrued and unpaid interest to, but excluding, the Redemption Date plus the &#8220;make-whole&#8221;
premium.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">&#160;</p>
